function HelpPage() {
  const [openKey, setOpenKey] = useState<string | null>(null)

  const toggle = (key: string) => setOpenKey(prev => prev === key ? null : key)

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background pb-8">
      <div className="flex items-center px-4 pt-4 pb-2">
        <button type="button" className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-muted"
          onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}>
          <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-foreground" />
        </button>
        <span className="flex-1 text-center text-xl font-bold text-foreground pr-10">帮助中心</span>
      </div>

      {/* 搜索提示 */}
      <div className="mx-4 mt-4 p-4 rounded-2xl bg-primary/5 border border-primary/20 flex items-center gap-3">
        <div className="i-mdi-headset text-3xl text-primary flex-shrink-0" />
        <div className="flex-1">
          <p className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground">遇到问题？</p>
          <p className="text-base text-muted-foreground">查看常见问题或联系客服</p>
        </div>
        <button type="button"
          className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none rounded-xl bg-primary"
          onClick={() => Taro.makePhoneCall({ phoneNumber: '400-000-0000' }).catch(() => {})}>
          <div className="px-3 py-2 text-xl font-bold text-white">联系客服</div>
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* 常见问题 */}
      {FAQ_GROUPS.map(group => (
        <div key={group.title} className="mx-4 mt-4 bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border overflow-hidden">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border">
            <div className={`${group.icon} text-2xl text-primary`} />
            <span className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground">{group.title}</span>
          </div>
          {group.items.map((item, idx) => {
            const key = `${group.title}-${idx}`
            const isOpen = openKey === key
            return (
              <div key={key} className="border-b border-border last:border-0">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-4"
                  onClick={() => toggle(key)}>
                  <span className="text-xl text-foreground flex-1 pr-2">{item.q}</span>
                  <div className={`i-mdi-chevron-down text-2xl text-muted-foreground transition-transform flex-shrink-0 ${isOpen ? 'rotate-180' : ''}`} />
                </div>
                {isOpen && (
                  <div className="px-4 pb-4">
                    <div className="p-3 bg-muted rounded-xl">
                      <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed">{item.a}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )
          })}
        </div>
      ))}

      {/* 底部联系方式 */}
      <div className="mx-4 mt-4 p-4 rounded-2xl bg-card border border-border">
        <p className="text-xl font-bold text-foreground mb-3">联系我们</p>
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">

          </div>

      </div>
    </div>

}

```
// @title 佣金明细
import { useState, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react'
import Taro from '@tarojs/taro'
import { getMyCommissions } from '@/db/api'
import type { Commission } from '@/db/types'
import { withRouteGuard } from '@/components/RouteGuard'

type Tab = 'all' | 'pending' | 'settled'

const statusLabel: Record<string, string> = {
  pending: '待结算', settled: '已结算', refunded: '已退款',
}
const statusColor: Record<string, string> = {
  pending: 'text-orange-500', settled: 'text-green-600', refunded: 'text-muted-foreground',
}

function CommissionDetailPage() {
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<Tab>('all')
  const [items, setItems] = useState<Commission[]>([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setItems(await getMyCommissions(0, 50))
    setLoading(false)
  }, [])
  useEffect(() => { load() }, [load])

  const filtered = items.filter(c => tab === 'all' || c.status === tab)

  const totalPending = items.filter(c => c.status === 'pending').reduce((s, c) => s + Number(c.amount), 0)
  const totalSettled = items.filter(c => c.status === 'settled').reduce((s, c) => s + Number(c.amount), 0)

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background pb-8">
      <div className="flex items-center px-4 pt-4 pb-2">
        <button type="button" className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-muted"
          onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}>
          <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-foreground" />
        </button>
        <span className="flex-1 text-center text-xl font-bold text-foreground pr-10">佣金明细</span>
      </div>

      {/* 汇总卡 */}
      <div className="mx-4 mt-3 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden" style={{ background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #C2410C, #EA580C)' }}>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 py-5">
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1 border-r border-white/20">
            <span className="text-3xl font-black text-white">¥{totalPending.toFixed(2)}</span>
            <span className="text-xl text-white/80">待结算</span>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1">
            <span className="text-3xl font-black text-white">¥{totalSettled.toFixed(2)}</span>
            <span className="text-xl text-white/80">已结算</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="px-4 pb-4">
          <button type="button"
            className="w-full flex items-center justify-center leading-none rounded-xl border border-white/40 bg-white/10"
            onClick={() => Taro.navigateTo({ url: '/pages/withdraw/index' })}>
            <div className="py-2 text-xl text-white font-bold">申请提现 →</div>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Tab */}
      <div className="flex mx-4 mt-4 bg-muted rounded-2xl p-1">
        {([['all', '全部'], ['pending', '待结算'], ['settled', '已结算']] as const).map(([key, label]) => (
          <div key={key}
            className={`flex-1 flex items-center justify-center py-2 rounded-xl text-xl font-bold transition ${tab === key ? 'bg-card text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`}
            onClick={() => setTab(key)}>
            {label}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="px-4 mt-4">
        {loading ? (
          <div className="flex justify-center py-16">
            <div className="i-mdi-loading text-4xl text-primary animate-spin" />
          </div>
        ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center py-16 gap-3">
            <div className="i-mdi-cash-remove text-6xl text-muted-foreground/30" />
            <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">暂无佣金记录</p>
            <p className="text-base text-muted-foreground text-center px-8">分享商品给好友，好友购买后即可获得佣金</p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          filtered.map(c => (
            <div key={c.id} className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border mb-3 p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className={`w-7 h-7 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${c.level === 1 ? 'bg-primary/10' : 'bg-blue-50'}`}>
                    <span className={`text-base font-bold ${c.level === 1 ? 'text-primary' : 'text-blue-600'}`}>L{c.level}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-xl text-foreground">
                    {c.level === 1 ? '直推佣金' : '二级佣金'}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <span className={`text-2xl font-black ${statusColor[c.status] || 'text-foreground'}`}>
                  +¥{Number(c.amount).toFixed(2)}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <span className="text-base text-muted-foreground">
                  {new Date(c.created_at).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}
                </span>
                <span className={`text-xl font-bold ${statusColor[c.status] || ''}`}>
                  {statusLabel[c.status] || c.status}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default withRouteGuard(CommissionDetailPage)

```

     1 // @title 商品详情
     2 import { useState, useCallback, useEffect, useMemo } from 'react'
     3 import Taro, { useDidShow, useShareAppMessage, useShareTimeline } from '@tarojs/taro'
     4 import { Image } from '@tarojs/components'
     5 import { getProductById, addToCart, getCartCount } from '@/db/api'
     6 import { updateCartBadge } from '@/utils/cartBadge'
     7 import type { Product } from '@/db/types'
     8 import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext'
     9 import { supabase } from '@/client/supabase'
    10 
    11 export default function ProductPage() {
    12   const { user } = useAuth()
    13   const id = useMemo(() => {
    14     const params = Taro.getCurrentInstance().router?.params
    15     return params?.id ? decodeURIComponent(params.id) : ''
    16   }, [])
    17   const [product, setProduct] = useState<Product | null>(null)
    18   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
    19   const [adding, setAdding] = useState(false)
    20   const [cartCount, setCartCount] = useState(0)
    21   const [myCode, setMyCode] = useState('')
    22 
    23   const load = useCallback(async () => {
    24     if (!id) return
    25     setLoading(true)
    26     const data = await getProductById(id)
    27     setProduct(data)
    28     setLoading(false)
    29   }, [id])
    30 
    31   const refreshCart = useCallback(async () => {
    32     if (!user) return
    33     setCartCount(await getCartCount())
    34     const { data } = await supabase.from('profiles').select('referral_code').maybeSingle()
    35     if (data?.referral_code) setMyCode(data.referral_code)
    36   }, [user])
    37 
    38   useEffect(() => { load(); refreshCart() }, [load, refreshCart])
    39   useDidShow(() => { refreshCart() })
    40 
    41   // 商品分享携带推广码，好友扫码→锁定为下线
    42   useShareAppMessage(() => ({
    43     title: product ? `${product.name} · 来店有喜江湖好物` : '来店有喜 · 武侠生活平台',
    44     path: `/pages/product/index?id=${encodeURIComponent(id)}${myCode ? `&ref=${myCode}` : ''}`,
    45   }))
    46   useShareTimeline(() => ({
    47     title: product ? `${product.name} · 来店有喜` : '来店有喜',
    48   }))
    49 
    50   const requireLogin = () => {
    51     if (!user) { Taro.navigateTo({ url: '/pages/login/index' }); return false }
    52     return true
    53   }
    54 
    55   const handleAddCart = async () => {
    56     if (!requireLogin() || !product) return
    57     setAdding(true)
    58     await addToCart(product.id, product.store_id)
    59     setAdding(false)
    60     setCartCount(prev => prev + 1)
    61     updateCartBadge()
    62     Taro.showToast({ title: '已加入行囊', icon: 'success' })
    63   }
    64 
    65   const handleBuyNow = async () => {
    66     if (!requireLogin() || !product) return
    67     setAdding(true)
    68     await addToCart(product.id, product.store_id)
    69     setAdding(false)
    70     updateCartBadge()
    71     Taro.navigateTo({ url: `/pages/payment/index?productId=${encodeURIComponent(product.id)}&total=${product.price}` })
    72   }
    73 
    74   if (loading) return (
    75     <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
    76       <div className="i-mdi-loading text-4xl text-primary animate-spin" />
    77     </div>
    78   )
    79   if (!product) return (
    80     <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
    81       <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">商品不存在</p>
    82     </div>
    83   )
    84 
    85   return (
    86     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background pb-28">
    87       {/* 商品图 + 顶部返回 + 购物车角标 */}
    88       <div className="relative">
    89         <Image src={product.image_url || ''} mode="aspectFill" className="w-full" style={{ height: '280px', display: 'block' }} />
    90         <button type="button"
    91           className="absolute top-3 left-4 w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-black/40 flex items-center justify-center"
    92           onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}>
    93           <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-white" />
    94         </button>
    95         {cartCount > 0 && (
    96           <div className="absolute top-3 right-4" onClick={() => Taro.switchTab({ url: '/pages/cart/index' })}>
    97             <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-black/40 flex items-center justify-center">
    98               <div className="i-mdi-shopping-outline text-2xl text-white" />
    99             </div>
   100             <div className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 min-w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-primary flex items-center justify-center px-1">

    setIsFav(newFav)
    setFavLoading(false)

export interface Commission {
  id: string
  order_id: string
  order_no: string
  beneficiary_id: string
  payer_id: string
  level: 1 | 2
  rank_at_time: string
  ratio: number
  pool_amount: number
  commission_amount: number
  b_coef: number
  status: CommissionStatus
  settle_at: string | null
  created_at: string
}

export interface PointsLog {
===
  return order
}

export async function getOrders(status?: OrderStatus, page = 0, limit = 20): Promise<Order[]> {
  let q = supabase.from('orders').select('*, order_items(*)')
    .order('created_at', { ascending: false }).range(page * limit, (page + 1) * limit - 1)
  if (status) q = q.eq('status', status)
  const { data } = await q
  return Array.isArray(data) ? data : []
}

    47   USING (beneficiary_id = auth.uid());

    49 -- points_logs：本人可查自己的流水
    50 CREATE POLICY "user_read_own_points_logs" ON public.points_logs
    51   FOR SELECT TO authenticated
    52   USING (user_id = auth.uid());
    53 
    54 -- 仅 service_role 可写（Edge Function 操作）
    55 CREATE POLICY "service_insert_commissions" ON public.commissions
    56   FOR INSERT TO service_role WITH CHECK (true);
    57 CREATE POLICY "service_update_commissions" ON public.commissions
    58   FOR UPDATE TO service_role USING (true);
    59 
    60 CREATE POLICY "service_insert_points_logs" ON public.points_logs
    61   FOR INSERT TO service_role WITH CHECK (true);
    62 
    63 -- 5. 索引
    64 CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_commissions_beneficiary ON public.commissions(beneficiary_id);
    65 CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_commissions_order ON public.commissions(order_id);
    66 CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_points_logs_user ON public.points_logs(user_id);
    67 CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_points_logs_order ON public.points_logs(order_id);
    68 


</observation>

[Read from /workspace/app-coobohaoham9/supabase/functions/distribute-commission/index.ts is successful.]
Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-coobohaoham9/supabase/functions/distribute-commission/index.ts:
     1 /**
     2  * distribute-commission Edge Function
     3  * V3 动态分佣系统
     4  * 让利池 = total_amount × 25%
     5  * L1佣金 = 让利池 × L1比例 × B系数（默认1.0）
     6  * L2佣金 = 让利池 × L2比例 × A系数（默认1.0）
     7  * 消费者积分 = 让利池 × 25%（按0.01元/积分换算）
     8  * 抽奖池 = 让利池 × 5%（暂记，未来接彩池）
     9  * 平台 ≥ 10%
    10  */
    11 import { createClient } from 'jsr:@supabase/supabase-js@2'
    12 
    13 const corsHeaders = {
    14   'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
    15   'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
    16 }
    17 
    18 // V3 段位分佣比例表
    19 const RANK_COMMISSION: Record<string, { l1: number; l2: number }> = {
    20   '江湖散修': { l1: 0.30, l2: 0.12 },
    21   '外门弟子': { l1: 0.36, l2: 0.15 },
    22   '内门弟子': { l1: 0.42, l2: 0.18 },
    23   '核心弟子': { l1: 0.48, l2: 0.21 },
    24   '长老':     { l1: 0.54, l2: 0.24 },
    25   '掌门':     { l1: 0.60, l2: 0.27 },
    26 }
    27 
    28 const PROFIT_POOL_RATIO = 0.25  // 让利池占订单金额
    29 const CONSUMER_POINTS_RATIO = 0.25  // 积分占让利池
    30 const LOTTERY_RATIO = 0.05          // 抽奖池占让利池
    31 const GOLD_BEAN_RATE = 0.01         // 1积分 = 0.01元
    32 
    33 function toFixed4(n: number) { return Math.round(n * 10000) / 10000 }
    34 
    35 Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => {
    36   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders })
    37 
    38   const supabase = createClient(Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!, Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!)
    39 
    40   try {
    41     const { order_id, order_no, payer_id, total_amount, referrer_id } = await req.json() as {
    42       order_id: string; order_no: string; payer_id: string
    43       total_amount: number; referrer_id: string | null
    44     }
    45 
    46     // 防重复：已分润的订单跳过
    47     const { data: ord } = await supabase.from('orders').select('commission_distributed').eq('id', order_id).maybeSingle()
    48     if (ord?.commission_distributed) {
    49       console.log('[distribute-commission] already distributed for', order_no)
    50       return Response.json({ success: true, skipped: true }, { headers: corsHeaders })
    51     }
    52 
    53     // 让利池
    54     const profitPool = toFixed4(total_amount * PROFIT_POOL_RATIO)
    55 
    56     // 查推荐链（L1 = referrer_id, L2 = referrer的推荐人）
    57     const commissionRows: any[] = []
    58     const pointsRows: any[] = []
    59 
    60     let l1UserId: string | null = referrer_id
    61     let l2UserId: string | null = null
    62 
    63     if (l1UserId) {
    64       const { data: l1Profile } = await supabase.from('profiles')
    65         .select('id, member_rank, referrer_id')
    66         .eq('id', l1UserId).maybeSingle()
    67 
    68       if (l1Profile) {
    69         const rankKey = l1Profile.member_rank ?? '江湖散修'
    70         const ratio = RANK_COMMISSION[rankKey] ?? RANK_COMMISSION['江湖散修']
    71         const l1Amount = toFixed4(profitPool * ratio.l1)
    72 
    73         commissionRows.push({
    74           order_id, order_no,
    75           beneficiary_id: l1UserId,
    76           payer_id,
    77           level: 1,
    78           rank_at_time: rankKey,
    79           ratio: ratio.l1,
    80           pool_amount: profitPool,
    81           commission_amount: l1Amount,
    82           b_coef: 1.0,
    83           status: 'pending',
    84         })
    85 
    86         // L2
    87         l2UserId = (l1Profile as any).referrer_id ?? null
    88         if (l2UserId && l2UserId !== payer_id) {
    89           const { data: l2Profile } = await supabase.from('profiles')
    90             .select('id, member_rank').eq('id', l2UserId).maybeSingle()
    91           if (l2Profile) {
    92             const rankKey2 = l2Profile.member_rank ?? '江湖散修'
    93             const ratio2 = RANK_COMMISSION[rankKey2] ?? RANK_COMMISSION['江湖散修']
    94             const l2Amount = toFixed4(profitPool * ratio2.l2)
    95 
    96             commissionRows.push({
    97               order_id, order_no,
    98               beneficiary_id: l2UserId,
    99               payer_id,
   100               level: 2,
   101               rank_at_time: rankKey2,
   102               ratio: ratio2.l2,
   103               pool_amount: profitPool,
   104               commission_amount: l2Amount,
   105               b_coef: 1.0,
   106               status: 'pending',
   107             })
   108           }
   109         }
   110       }
   111     }
   112 
   113     // 消费者积分（购物返9%）
   114     const consumerPointsYuan = toFixed4(profitPool * CONSUMER_POINTS_RATIO)
   115     const consumerPoints = Math.floor(consumerPointsYuan / GOLD_BEAN_RATE) // 积分数量（整数）
   116 
   117     if (consumerPoints > 0) {
   118       // 查当前积分余额
   119       const { data: payerProfile } = await supabase.from('profiles').select('points').eq('id', payer_id).maybeSingle()
   120       const currentPoints = payerProfile?.points ?? 0
   121       // 每日上限200积分（简单累计，生产环境需要按天分组查）
   122       const balanceAfter = currentPoints + consumerPoints
   123 
   124       // 更新积分
   125       await supabase.from('profiles').update({ points: balanceAfter }).eq('id', payer_id)
   126 
   127       pointsRows.push({
   128         user_id: payer_id,
   129         order_id,
   130         type: 'purchase_earn',
   131         delta: consumerPoints,
   132         balance_after: balanceAfter,
   133         remark: `订单${order_no}购物返积分`,
   134       })
   135     }
   136 
   137     // 写佣金记录
   138     if (commissionRows.length > 0) {
   139       await supabase.from('commissions').insert(commissionRows)
   140     }
   141     // 写积分流水
   142     if (pointsRows.length > 0) {
   143       await supabase.from('points_logs').insert(pointsRows)
   144     }
   145 
   146     // 标记已分润
   147     await supabase.from('orders').update({ commission_distributed: true }).eq('id', order_id)
   148 
   149     return Response.json({
   150       success: true,
   151       profit_pool: profitPool,
   152       l1_commission: commissionRows.find(c => c.level === 1)?.commission_amount ?? 0,
   153       l2_commission: commissionRows.find(c => c.level === 2)?.commission_amount ?? 0,
   154       consumer_points: consumerPoints,
   155     }, { headers: corsHeaders })
   156 
   157   } catch (err: any) {
   158     console.error('[distribute-commission]', err)
   159     return Response.json({ error: err?.message ?? '内部错误' }, { status: 500, headers: corsHeaders })
   160   }
   161 })

    65 -- 4. 段位升级规则（用于前端展示进度）
    66 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.get_rank_progress(p_user_id uuid)
    67 RETURNS jsonb LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER AS $$
    68 DECLARE
    69   v_profile RECORD;
    70   v_direct_count int;
    71   v_total_gmv numeric;
    72   v_next_rank text;
    73   v_progress numeric;
    74   v_target int;
    75 BEGIN
    76   SELECT member_rank, points, balance INTO v_profile FROM public.profiles WHERE id = p_user_id;
    77   -- 统计直接下级数
    78   SELECT count(*) INTO v_direct_count FROM public.profiles WHERE referrer_id = p_user_id;
    79   -- 统计个人GMV（已完成订单）
    80   SELECT COALESCE(sum(total_amount), 0) INTO v_total_gmv FROM public.orders
    81   WHERE user_id = p_user_id AND status NOT IN ('cancelled', 'after_sale');
    82 
    83   -- 段位进度规则（简化版）
    84   CASE v_profile.member_rank
    85     WHEN '江湖散修' THEN v_next_rank := '外门弟子'; v_target := 3; v_progress := LEAST(v_direct_count::numeric / 3, 1);
    86     WHEN '外门弟子' THEN v_next_rank := '内门弟子'; v_target := 10; v_progress := LEAST(v_direct_count::numeric / 10, 1);
    87     WHEN '内门弟子' THEN v_next_rank := '核心弟子'; v_target := 30; v_progress := LEAST(v_direct_count::numeric / 30, 1);
    88     WHEN '核心弟子' THEN v_next_rank := '长老'; v_target := 100; v_progress := LEAST(v_direct_count::numeric / 100, 1);
    89     WHEN '长老' THEN v_next_rank := '掌门'; v_target := 300; v_progress := LEAST(v_direct_count::numeric / 300, 1);
    90     ELSE v_next_rank := '已是最高段位'; v_target := 0; v_progress := 1;
    91   END CASE;
    92 
    93   RETURN jsonb_build_object(
    94     'current_rank', v_profile.member_rank,
    95     'next_rank', v_next_rank,
    96     'direct_count', v_direct_count,
    97     'target_count', v_target,
    98     'progress', v_progress,
    99     'total_gmv', v_total_gmv,
   100     'points', v_profile.points,
   101     'balance', v_profile.balance
   102   );
   103 END;
   104 $$;

     2 -- 1. profiles 新增推广码与上级字段
     3 ALTER TABLE public.profiles
     4   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS referral_code text UNIQUE,
     5   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS referrer_id uuid REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL;
     6 
     7 -- 为已有用户生成推广码（6位大写字母+数字）
     8 UPDATE public.profiles
     9 SET referral_code = upper(substr(replace(gen_random_uuid()::text, '-', ''), 1, 6))
    10 WHERE referral_code IS NULL;
    11 
    12 -- 新用户注册触发器：自动生成推广码
    13 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.handle_new_user_referral()
    14 RETURNS TRIGGER LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER AS $$
    15 BEGIN
    16   IF NEW.referral_code IS NULL THEN
    17     NEW.referral_code := upper(substr(replace(gen_random_uuid()::text, '-', ''), 1, 6));
    18   END IF;
    19   RETURN NEW;
    20 END;
    21 $$;
    22 
    23 DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS on_profile_referral_code ON public.profiles;
    24 CREATE TRIGGER on_profile_referral_code
    25   BEFORE INSERT ON public.profiles
    26   FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION public.handle_new_user_referral();
    27 
    28 -- 2. orders 新增服务类型
    29 DO $$ BEGIN
    30   CREATE TYPE service_type AS ENUM ('dine_in', 'self_pickup', 'delivery');
    31 EXCEPTION WHEN duplicate_object THEN NULL; END $$;
    32 
    33 ALTER TABLE public.orders
    34   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS service_type service_type NOT NULL DEFAULT 'delivery';
    35 
    36 -- 3. RPC：绑定上级（注册时调用，幂等）
    37 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.bind_referrer(p_referral_code text)
    38 RETURNS jsonb LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER AS $$
    39 DECLARE
    40   v_referrer RECORD;
    41   v_self_code text;
    42 BEGIN
    43   -- 查自己的推广码，避免自绑
    44   SELECT referral_code INTO v_self_code FROM public.profiles WHERE id = auth.uid();
    45   IF v_self_code = upper(trim(p_referral_code)) THEN
    46     RETURN jsonb_build_object('success', false, 'error', '不能绑定自己的推广码');
    47   END IF;
    48 
    49   -- 查推广人
    50   SELECT id, referral_code INTO v_referrer FROM public.profiles WHERE referral_code = upper(trim(p_referral_code));
    51   IF NOT FOUND THEN
    52     RETURN jsonb_build_object('success', false, 'error', '推广码不存在');
    53   END IF;
    54 
    55   -- 幂等：已绑定则跳过
    56   IF EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles WHERE id = auth.uid() AND referrer_id IS NOT NULL) THEN
    57     RETURN jsonb_build_object('success', true, 'message', '已绑定');
    58   END IF;

# 来店有喜 V3 终极版：积分奖励与分销分佣机制财务安全与防亏损分析报告

本报告针对“来店有喜”小程序中实施的 **V3 动态分佣系统与积分奖励机制** 进行深度数学建模与财务安全评估。通过剖析系统源码（尤其是 `distribute-commission` 边缘函数与数据库设计），评估平台在不同分销段位下的利润留存情况，指出潜在的亏损漏洞，并提出针对性的优化建议。

---

## 一、 核心结论：平台存在严重的结构性亏损风险

**是的，在目前的设计下，当分销商晋升到高段位（“长老”和“掌门”）时，平台将面临结构性的财务亏损（资金穿仓）。**

具体而言：
1. **中低段位（核心弟子及以下）**：平台能够保持正向盈利，每笔交易能留存让利池的 $1\% \sim 28\%$（折合订单金额的 $0.25\% \sim 7\%$）。
2. **高段位（长老、掌门）**：总拨出比例分别达到了让利池的 **$108\%$** 和 **$117\%$**。这意味着**每产生一笔高段位分销订单，平台不仅没有盈利，反而需要从自身资金池中额外垫付让利池金额的 $8\% \sim 17\%$（折合订单总额的 $2\% \sim 4.25\%$）**。
3. **商家侧毛利倒挂风险**：目前让利池硬编码为订单金额的 $25\%$。对于本地生活商家而言，扣除 $25\%$ 的佣金扣点极高，这会导致优质商家流失。若强行降低扣点而保持分润公式不变，亏损将成倍放大。

---

## 二、 积分与分佣机制的数学建模剖析

根据系统核心代码 `supabase/functions/distribute-commission/index.ts`，资金分配公式如下：

*   **订单总金额**：$A$
*   **让利池 (Profit Pool)**：$P = A \times 25\%$
*   **消费者积分返利**：$Points = P \times 25\% \div 0.01$ (等值于现金 $P \times 25\% = A \times 6.25\%$)
*   **平台抽奖池 (预留)**：$L = P \times 5\% = A \times 1.25\%$
*   **分销级别**：直推 (L1) 与 间推 (L2)

### 1. 各段位分佣比例及平台利润留存表

平台拨出总额包含：`L1佣金 + L2佣金 + 消费者积分 (25%) + 抽奖池 (5%)`。

| 推荐人/间推人段位 | L1 佣金比例 (占 P) | L2 佣金比例 (占 P) | 佣金小计 (占 P) | 其他拨出 (占 P) <br>*(积分25% + 彩池5%)* | **总拨出比例 (占 P)** | **平台留存比例 (占 P)** | **平台留存折合订单金额 (占 A)** | **财务安全性评估** |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **江湖散修** | $30\%$ | $12\%$ | $42\%$ | $30\%$ | **$72\%$** | **$+28\%$** | $+7.00\%$ | **安全**（高额盈利） |
| **外门弟子** | $36\%$ | $15\%$ | $51\%$ | $30\%$ | **$81\%$** | **$+19\%$** | $+4.75\%$ | **安全**（适度盈利） |
| **内门弟子** | $42\%$ | $18\%$ | $60\%$ | $30\%$ | **$90\%$** | **$+10\%$** | $+2.50\%$ | **安全**（微利状态） |
| **核心弟子** | $48\%$ | $21\%$ | $69\%$ | $30\%$ | **$99\%$** | **$+1\%$** | $+0.25\%$ | **临界点**（近乎无利） |
| **长老** | $54\%$ | $24\%$ | $78\%$ | $30\%$ | **$108\%$** | **$-8\%$** | $-2.00\%$ | 🔴 **亏损**（每单倒贴 2%） |
| **掌门** | $60\%$ | $27\%$ | $87\%$ | $30\%$ | **$117\%$** | **$-117\%$** | $-4.25\%$ | 🔴 **严重亏损**（倒贴 4.25%） |

### 2. 极端亏损案例测算
假设一位“掌门”用户 A 推荐了另一位“掌门”用户 B，用户 B 引导消费者购买了一笔价值 **$1000$ 元** 的武侠文创商品：
*   **让利池**：$P = 1000 \times 25\% = 250$ 元
*   **L1 佣金 (用户 B 获得)**：$250 \times 60\% = 150$ 元
*   **L2 佣金 (用户 A 获得)**：$250 \times 27\% = 67.5$ 元
*   **消费者购物返积分**：$250 \times 25\% = 62.5$ 元 (折合 $6250$ 金豆，可 1:1 抵扣付款或通过提现通道变现)
*   **抽奖池积攒**：$250 \times 5\% = 12.5$ 元
*   **分配总额**：$150 + 67.5 + 62.5 + 12.5 = 292.5$ 元
*   **平台损益**：$250 \text{ (商家让利)} - 292.5 \text{ (平台实际拨出)} = -42.5$ 元。
*   **结果**：平台在该笔订单中**净亏损 42.5 元**。

---

## 三、 导致平台亏损的四大核心财务漏洞

1.  **高段位佣金拨出无封顶机制（致命伤）**
    目前的动态分润直接将 L1 与 L2 比例相加。当裂变链条中出现双“掌门”或“长老+掌门”时，总佣金比例高达 $87\%$，加上消费者返点 $25\%$ 与彩池 $5\%$，总拨出比例达 $117\%$，彻底击穿 $100\%$ 的安全线。
2.  **积分（金豆）具备 100% 的现金等值性，无“消泡沫”机制**
    系统中积分以 $0.01$ 元/分换算，不仅可以直接抵扣付款，还能在提现页面以 `100 豆 = 1 元` 的比例直接提现。这意味着积分具有完全的现金负债属性，而非一般的“优惠券”或“商城兑换券”，属于硬性刚兑，极大增加了平台现金流压力。
3.  **商户让利比例（扣点）硬编码，缺乏弹性**
    让利池直接以 $25\%$ 订单额计算。本地生活（餐饮、娱乐、门票）的行业平均利润率通常在 $15\% \sim 30\%$ 之间，强制扣点 $25\%$ 相当于让商家将所有净利润甚至部分成本交出。如果未来为了招商妥协，将平台扣点降到 $10\%$ 或 $15\%$，而分销比例不作等比例压缩，平台每单的亏损额度将进一步扩大数倍。
4.  **混合支付中的“代币超发”与“双重抵扣”**
    如果用户使用“金豆+微信混合支付”，被消耗的金豆本应作为债务销账，但目前下单时的总额 $total\_amount$ 依然以全额计算并投入分佣池，从而导致“虚假交易额”参与分佣，产生了二次套利空间。

---

## 四、 针对性的财务安全与机制优化建议

为了确保“来店有喜”小程序能长效健康运转，同时保留“武侠国潮”分销的裂变魅力，提出以下优化建议：

### 1. 实行“级差分销”或“团队差额制”，取代简单的“固定叠加制”
*   **方案**：L1 和 L2 的佣金比例之和必须设置一个绝对上限（例如不超过让利池的 $60\%$）。
*   **设计**：采用**级差机制**。例如，极高段位的佣金是由于其团队带来的级差奖励。如果下级段位已经很高，上级只能拿极低的级差代数奖，而非直接累加。
*   **快速修复**：在 `distribute-commission` 函数中引入平台保护锁：
    $$\text{Total\_Commission} = \min(L1\_Amount + L2\_Amount, \ P \times 60\%)$$
    确保佣金拨出比例永远封顶在 $60\%$，为积分 ($25\%$)、彩池 ($5\%$) 和平台留存 ($15\%$) 留出绝对安全空间。

### 2. 剥离积分（金豆）的“现金刚兑”属性
*   **建议**：**积分只能用于“珍宝阁”兑换非刚兑性代金券、限定周边，或按比例抵扣消费，严禁直接提现。**
*   **金豆贬值与手续费**：如果保留提现，提现需要收取高额的“江湖税”（如 $10\% \sim 20\%$ 的提现手续费），用于销毁泡沫。
*   **抵扣上限**：在消费抵扣时，限制单笔订单最高只能用金豆抵扣 $10\% \sim 20\%$，防止纯金豆支付（薅羊毛导致商户货款无法用人民币结算）。

### 3. 引入“商家自主让利比例”机制 (Flexible Margin)
*   **方案**：废除硬编码的 $25\%$ 让利池。在 `stores` 表或 `products` 表中增加 `profit_sharing_ratio`（让利比例）字段，由商家根据自身毛利空间自主设置（如餐饮设置 $12\%$，文创设置 $30\%$）。
*   **适配分佣**：分佣池 $P$ 动态计算：$P = A \times \text{profit\_sharing\_ratio}$。分销商赚取的绝对金额随着商家让利空间动态波动。这既能吸引低毛利高频次的刚需商家入驻，又能保护平台不垫资。

### 4. 引入 B 系数（活跃度）与 A 系数（风控锁）的真正作用
*   代码中已经预留了 `b_coef`（消费者活跃度系数，默认 1.0）。
*   **建议**：激活该系数。对于不活跃、无自主 UGC 发布、无每日签到的“僵尸推广员”，其 `b_coef` 降为 $0.5$ 甚至更低。
*   当检测到团队存在“对撞套利”（如注册一堆小号左手倒右手）时，通过 A 系数自动判定异常，将分佣比例动态压缩，实行风控阻断。

### 5. 扣除代币支付部分后再计算分佣 (Net Commissioning)
*   如果一笔 100 元的订单，用户使用了价值 30 元的金豆抵扣，微信实际支付 70 元。
*   分佣让利池应基于**现金实际支付额 (70元)** 计算，而非总额 (100元)。
*   这能彻底斩断“金豆购买商品 $\rightarrow$ 产生新积分 $\rightarrow$ 产生新佣金 $\rightarrow$ 再次购买”的无限循环套利螺旋。
